<ul class=wp-block-list>

<li>The company focuses on new tech, like cloud computing and cybersecurity.</li>
<li>It plans to collaborate with other big tech companies so that it can get more brand value.</li>
<li>The company has little debt and a lot of cash, which means they’re financially stable and can handle tough times or invest in new opportunities.</li>
</ul>

<h3 class=wp-block-heading><span id=Bear_Case><strong>Bear Case</strong></span></h3>

<li>With so many competitors, there’s pressure to lower prices, which can reduce profits.</li>

<li>If Happiest Minds acquires other companies or forms new partnerships, there might be difficulties in merging and making the most of these deals.</li>
